And the sign is that the ankle is swollen, and it tents forward at the part where it is dislocated; the resetting should be easy, and one must gently extend the limb with their hands when it is only slightly moved.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is dislocated entirely, one must make the patient sit up straight, and have assistants hold them firmly by the leg above the ankle; then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, then your left hand twice, then lift it upwards, and place the foot firmly in its proper position; repeat this two times as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns to place, that is good. If not, begin the procedure again, for it will return. And if it cannot be returned thus, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and firmly plant a stake in the earth between their thighs, and tie cloths around so as not to injure the patient; then have assistants hold the thigh, and another assistant extend the foot with their hands or use a rope tied to the neck of the foot; then each assistant should pull evenly, and the stake should always be between the patient's thighs to keep them steady while they are stretched; then the surgeon should place his hands evenly on the dislocation, and an assistant hold the healthy leg below it, and the dislocation will quickly return.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is ready, then place the plaster and bandages on it, bind it tightly, and tie the foot to the leg, and guard the nerves that are behind the ankle so that the binding is not too tight; then leave it for two or three days, and if the binding loosens, bind it again; then untie it on the third or fourth day, and forbid the patient from walking for four days; and if they walk before this time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"If inflammation occurs around the dislocation, you must calm it as we have described elsewhere until it is healed."
des dois	Chapter on dislocations of the fingers
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	"When the fingers are dislocated, they should be gently extended without force, which is easy to do."
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any of the joints of the back of the foot, then you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or on a table, completely upright, and place your foot on what opens from these joints, then press down on your foot with great force until it returns; and when it is even and nothing opens anymore, then place two-legged stool under the sole of the foot, then bind it tightly and leave it for three days, then untie it; and let them rest until they are healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Chapter on wounds accompanied by dislocations
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with dislocation and one wishes to reset it, often the patient dies: therefore, do not be presumptuous in its treatment unless you are wise in the art and have practiced it extensively, and are compassionate and careful, not hasty; at first, apply soothing ointments for hot inflammation, and leave the patient in God's hands if there is no hope of recovery. But if there is hope, then reset the limb to its place before the inflammation becomes worse. Once the limb is in place, administer ointments to cool inflammation, and treat the wound as necessary with drying ointments. And if with dislocation there is fracture or crushed small bones, set them and do as we have said for simple fractures. Guard against fearing, as I have said, for this leads to sin according to your Creator, and harms your soul and body.
Amen	Amen
